NCR_helios_category = {

	NCR_repair_helios_fantastic = {

		icon = generic_oppression
		
		available = {
			NCR = { owns_state = 417 }
			NCR = { controls_state = 417 }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 417
		}

		cost = 50

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 33
		}

		visible = {
			NCR = { owns_state = 417 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = NCR_helios_brotherhood}
			OR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NCR_helios_fantastic}}
			OR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NCR_helios_followers}}
		}

		is_good = yes

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = debug_logs }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] NCR_repair_helios_fantastic (decision) complete entered"
			}
			set_country_flag = NCR_helios_fantastic
			
			417 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 5
			add_building_construction = {
					type = electricity_generator
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}	
				add_resource = {
					type = fuel
					amount = 15
				}	
				add_resource = {
					type = electricity
					amount = 15
				}				  
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = debug_logs }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] NCR_repair_helios_fantastic (decision) complete exited"
			}
		}
	}

NCR_heavytroops_focus_category = {
	NCR_armourexperiment_focus = {
		icon = GFX_decision_oppression
		
		available = {
			NCR = { owns_state = 253 }
			NCR = { controls_state = 253 }
			hidden_trigger = { NCR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_spawned_armorexperiment } } }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 253
		}

		cost = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		visible = {
			NCR = { owns_state = 253 }
			NCR = { has_completed_focus = ncr_armourexperiment }
			hidden_trigger = { NCR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_spawned_armorexperiment } } }
		}

		is_good = yes

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = debug_logs }

ncr_revolts = {
	seek_peace = {
		visible = {
			has_variable = revolt_progress
			tag = NCR
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { # AI will do it after 3 events have fired
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				check_variable = { var = revolt_progress value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = debug_logs }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] seek_peace (decision) complete entered"
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PHR
						is_in_faction_with = PHR
					}
				}
				white_peace = NCR
			}
			hidden_effect = { PHR = { country_event = { id = nf_ncr.40 days = 10 } } } # Dissolution of the Federation
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { revolt_progress = 1 } }
				add_political_power = -50 # wuss
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { revolt_progress = 2 } }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_development days = 60 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = PHR
							is_in_faction_with = PHR
						}
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_payments days = 60 }
				}
				add_political_power = -20 # Slightly less of a wuss
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { revolt_progress = 2 } }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_development days = 90 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = PHR
							is_in_faction_with = PHR
						}
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_payments days = 90 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { revolt_progress = 3 } }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_development days = 180 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = PHR
							is_in_faction_with = PHR
						}
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_payments days = 180 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { revolt_progress = 4 } }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_development days = 360 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = PHR
							is_in_faction_with = PHR
						}
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_payments days = 360 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { revolt_progress = 5 } }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_development days = 720 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = PHR
							is_in_faction_with = PHR
						}
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ncr_revolts_payments days = 720 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = debug_logs }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] seek_peace (decision) complete exited"
			}
		}
	}
}

# Setting the pulse for each district
@sr_pulse = 90
@redding_pulse = 80
@diablo_pulse = 90
@dayglow_pulse = 70
@rapids_pulse = 65
@boneyard_pulse = 80
@divide_pulse = 100
@southern_mojave_pulse = 70
@central_mojave_pulse = 60
@northern_mojave_pulse = 65
@baja_pulse = 65
@ranchers_pulse = 110
@nevada_pulse = 90
@junktown_pulse = 120

ncr_raider_trouble = {
	# Planning at https://docs.google.com/document/d/1XNZdjfPeu2SCb2QZ5lXqY9FUXj9XMaXnS_5jOVhVzc0
	## Santa Rose ##
	# Global Interactions
	raider_pulse_sr = {
		priority = 25
		activation = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { sr_intensity = 0 } }
			any_owned_state = {
				sr_raid_district = yes
			}
			OR = {
				tag = NCR
				is_puppet_of = NCR
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = @sr_pulse
		is_good = no
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { sr_intensity = 0 } }
				set_global_flag = sr_district_pacified
				custom_effect_tooltip = sr_district_pacified
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { sr_intensity = 1 } }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						random_owned_state = {
							limit = { sr_raid_district = yes }
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 1
							}
							ROOT = {
								random_owned_state = {
									limit = {
										sr_raid_district = yes
										NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = infrastructure
										damage = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {}
				}
				random_list = {
					32 = {
						add_to_variable = { var = sr_intensity value = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_increases
					}
					68 = {}	
				}
			}
			else_if = {

			NOT = { has_global_flag = sr_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sr_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_sr
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { sr_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_sr }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_sr
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sr_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { sr_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { sr_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { sr_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { sr_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { sr_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_sr
		}
	}

	## Redding ##
	# Global Interactions
	raider_pulse_redding = {
		priority = 23
		activation = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { redding_intensity = 0 } }
			any_owned_state = {
				redding_raid_district = yes
			}
			OR = {
				tag = NCR
				is_puppet_of = NCR
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = @redding_pulse
		is_good = no
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_intensity = 0 } }
				set_global_flag = redding_district_pacified
				custom_effect_tooltip = redding_district_pacified
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_intensity = 1 } }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						random_owned_state = {
							limit = { redding_raid_district = yes }
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 1
							}
							ROOT = {
								random_owned_state = {
									limit = {
										redding_raid_district = yes
										NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = infrastructure
										damage = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {}
				}
				random_list = {
					32 = {
						add_to_variable = { var = redding_intensity value = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_increases
					}
					68 = {}	
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_intensity = 2 } }

							limit = { redding_raid_district = yes }

								damage = 2

										damage = 2
									}

					}

				}

							redding_raid_district = yes
							industrial_complex > 0
						}

								}

										}

											type = industrial_complex
											damage = 0.3
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}

					}
				}

					}

				}

								damage_building = {
									type = arms_factory
									damage = 0.9
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										dockyard > 0
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = dockyard
										damage = 0.9
									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									random_owned_state = {
										limit = {
											redding_raid_district = yes
											arms_factory > 0
											NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
										}
										damage_building = {
											type = arms_factory
											damage = 0.9
										}
										if = {
											limit = {
												dockyard > 0
											}
											damage_building = {
												type = dockyard
												damage = 0.9
											}
										}
										ROOT = {
											random_owned_state = {
												limit = {
													redding_raid_district = yes
													arms_factory > 0
													NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
													NOT = { state = PREV.PREV.PREV.PREV }
												}
												damage_building = {
													type = arms_factory
													damage = 0.9
												}
												if = {
													limit = {
														dockyard > 0
													}
													damage_building = {
														type = dockyard
														damage = 0.9
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						25 = {}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					60 = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.3 } }
					25 = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.2 } }
					15 = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.2 } }
				}
				random_list = {
					52 = {
						add_to_variable = { var = redding_intensity value = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_increases
					}
					48 = {}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_intensity = 10 } }
				#secession_raid_crisis = yes # Calls the scripted effect to launch a secession crisis
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = "Something has gone really fucking wrong - tell @HappyNTH"
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {

		}

	enlargen_garrison_redding = {
		priority = 22
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				redding_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = redding_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = redding_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_redding
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { redding_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_redding }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_redding
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = redding_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { redding_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { redding_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { redding_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { redding_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { redding_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_redding
		}

	enlargen_garrison_diablo = {
		priority = 20
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				diablo_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = diablo_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = diablo_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_diablo
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { diablo_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_diablo }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_diablo
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = diablo_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { diablo_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { diablo_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { diablo_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { diablo_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { diablo_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_diablo
		}
	}

			has_200_weapons = yes
		}
		cost = 20
		days_remove = 20
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_diablo
			subtract_from_variable = { ranger_deployments = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_deployment
			add_manpower = -200
			remove_200_weapons = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }
				subtract_from_variable = { diablo_intenisty = 6 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity
			}
			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { diablo_intenisty = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
			}
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_diablo
		}

	enlargen_garrison_dayglow = {
		priority = 18
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				dayglow_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = dayglow_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = dayglow_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_dayglow
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { dayglow_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = dayglow_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow
		}
	}

				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 3 } }

				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action

			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow

					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { dayglow_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow
		}

		days_re_enable = 60

			    value = -200

		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }

							}

								subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
						}
					}

							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 3 }

							}

								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_4_intensity
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_mil
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund } }
						random_list = {

							}
							35 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_list = {
							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}

	call_rangers_dayglow = {
		priority = 18
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				dayglow_raid_district = yes
			}

			}

			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow }
			}
		}
		cost = 20
		days_remove = 20
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow
			add_autonomy_score = {
			    value = -400
			    localization = called_in_ncr_rangers
			}
			NCR = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.7 } }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_rangers } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = if_ncr_agrees_rangers
				effect_tooltip = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 6 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 5 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_rangers
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_rangers } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 6 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { dayglow_intenisty = 5 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ncr_refuses_rangers
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_dayglow
		}

	enlargen_garrison_rapids = {
		priority = 16
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				rapids_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = rapids_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = rapids_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_rapids
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { rapids_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_rapids }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_rapids
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = rapids_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { rapids_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { rapids_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { rapids_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { rapids_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { rapids_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_rapids
		}
	}

	arm_civilians_rapids = {
		priority = 16
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				rapids_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = rapids_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = rapids_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_rapids
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { rapids_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_rapids }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_rapids
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = rapids_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { rapids_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { rapids_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_rapids
		}
	}

				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 1 } }
				has_political_power > 39
			}

				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 2 } }
				has_political_power > 79
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 3 } }
				has_political_power > 159
			}

				limit = { check_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 4 } }
				has_political_power > 319
			}
		}

		days_re_enable = 60

					add_political_power = -80
					add_to_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 3 } }

					add_to_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 4 } }
					add_political_power = -320
					add_to_variable = { rapids_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen

			}

	enlargen_garrison_boneyard = {
		priority = 14
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				boneyard_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = boneyard_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = boneyard_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_boneyard
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { boneyard_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = boneyard_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard
		}
	}

	arm_civilians_boneyard = {
		priority = 14
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				boneyard_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = boneyard_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = boneyard_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_boneyard
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { boneyard_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = boneyard_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard
		}
	}

		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost - purposefully one under so can be selected at that threshold
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = boneyard_merc_use } }
				has_political_power > 19
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 } }
				has_political_power > 39
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 2 } }
				has_political_power > 79
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 3 } }
				has_political_power > 159
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 4 } }
				has_political_power > 319
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_pp_boneyard
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { boneyard_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = merc_limit_boneyard
				NOT = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 40
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = boneyard_merc_use } }
					add_political_power = -20
					set_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 } }
					add_political_power = -40
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 2 } }
					add_political_power = -80
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 3 } }
					add_political_power = -160
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 4 } }
					add_political_power = -320
					add_to_variable = { boneyard_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 2 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
				}
				25 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { boneyard_intenisty = 3 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
				} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_boneyard
		}
	}

								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_4_intensity
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {

			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }

						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund } }

								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {

	raider_pulse_divide = {
		priority = 13
		activation = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { divide_intensity = 0 } }
			any_owned_state = {

			}

				tag = NCR
				is_puppet_of = NCR
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = @divide_pulse
		is_good = no
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

							}

									}

										type = infrastructure
										damage = 1
									}

				}

	enlargen_garrison_divide = {
		priority = 12
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				divide_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = divide_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = divide_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_divide
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { divide_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = divide_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { divide_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
		}
	}
	attempt_integration_divide = {
		priority = 12
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				divide_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = divide_district_pacified }

			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide }
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 100
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				60 = {} # No effect
				35 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 2 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
				}
				5 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 3 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
		}
	}
	arm_civilians_divide = {
		priority = 12
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				divide_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = divide_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = divide_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_divide
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { divide_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = divide_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { divide_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
		}
	}
	employ_mercs_divide = {
		priority = 12
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				divide_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = divide_district_pacified }
			has_global_flag = ncr_chose_big_jim
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost - purposefully one under so can be selected at that threshold
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = divide_merc_use } }
				has_political_power > 19
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 } }
				has_political_power > 39
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 2 } }
				has_political_power > 79
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 3 } }
				has_political_power > 159
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 4 } }
				has_political_power > 319
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_pp_divide
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity

			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 40
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = divide_merc_use } }

					set_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 } }
					add_political_power = -40
					add_to_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 2 } }
					add_political_power = -80
					add_to_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 3 } }
					add_political_power = -160
					add_to_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { divide_merc_use = 4 } }
					add_political_power = -320
					add_to_variable = { divide_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 2 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
				}
				25 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { divide_intenisty = 3 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
				} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_divide
		}

	enlargen_garrison_southern_mojave = {
		priority = 10
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				southern_mojave_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = southern_mojave_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = southern_mojave_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_southern_mojave
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_southern_mojave }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_southern_mojave
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = southern_mojave_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { southern_mojave_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { southern_mojave_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { southern_mojave_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { southern_mojave_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_southern_mojave
		}

				southern_mojave_raid_district = yes
			}

				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}

				NOT = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_southern_mojave }
			}
		}

		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_southern_mojave

					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { southern_mojave_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { southern_mojave_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_southern_mojave
		}

	## Central Mojave ##
	# Global Interactions
	raider_pulse_central_mojave = {
		priority = 9
		activation = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 0 } }
			any_owned_state = {
				central_mojave_raid_district = yes
			}
			OR = {
				tag = NCR
				is_puppet_of = NCR
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = @central_mojave_pulse
		is_good = no
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 0 } }
				set_global_flag = central_mojave_district_pacified
				custom_effect_tooltip = central_mojave_district_pacified
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 1 } }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						random_owned_state = {
							limit = { central_mojave_raid_district = yes }
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 1
							}
							ROOT = {
								random_owned_state = {
									limit = {
										central_mojave_raid_district = yes
										NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = infrastructure
										damage = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {}
				}
				random_list = {
					32 = {
						add_to_variable = { var = central_mojave_intensity value = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_increases
					}
					68 = {}	
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 2 } }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						random_owned_state = {
							limit = { central_mojave_raid_district = yes }
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 2
							}
							ROOT = {
								random_owned_state = {
									limit = {
										central_mojave_raid_district = yes
										NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = infrastructure
										damage = 2
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							central_mojave_raid_district = yes
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
							random_owned_state = {
								limit = {
									central_mojave_raid_district = yes
									industrial_complex > 0
								}
								damage_building = {
									type = industrial_complex
									damage = 0.3
								}
								ROOT = {
									random_owned_state = {
										limit = {
											central_mojave_raid_district = yes
											industrial_complex > 0
											NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
										}
										damage_building = {
											type = industrial_complex
											damage = 0.3
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						25 = {}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					42 = {
						add_to_variable = { var = central_mojave_intensity value = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_increases
					}
					58 = {}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 3 }
				}
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						random_owned_state = {
							limit = { central_mojave_raid_district = yes }
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 2
							}
							ROOT = {
								random_owned_state = {
									limit = {
										central_mojave_raid_district = yes
										NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = infrastructure
										damage = 2
									}
									ROOT = {
										random_owned_state = {
											limit = {
												central_mojave_raid_district = yes
												NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
												NOT = { state = PREV.PREV.PREV.PREV }
											}
											damage_building = {
												type = infrastructure
												damage = 2
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							central_mojave_raid_district = yes
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
							random_owned_state = {
								limit = {
									central_mojave_raid_district = yes

													industrial_complex > 0
													NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
													NOT = { state = PREV.PREV.PREV.PREV }
												}
												damage_building = {
													type = industrial_complex
													damage = 0.9
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						25 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							central_mojave_raid_district = yes
							arms_factory > 0
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
							random_owned_state = {
								limit = {
									central_mojave_raid_district = yes
									arms_factory > 0
								}
								damage_building = {
									type = arms_factory
									damage = 0.9
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										dockyard > 0
									}
									damage_building = {
										type = dockyard
										damage = 0.9
									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									random_owned_state = {
										limit = {
											central_mojave_raid_district = yes
											arms_factory > 0
											NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
										}
										damage_building = {
											type = arms_factory
											damage = 0.9
										}
										if = {
											limit = {
												dockyard > 0
											}
											damage_building = {
												type = dockyard
												damage = 0.9
											}
										}
										ROOT = {
											random_owned_state = {
												limit = {
													central_mojave_raid_district = yes
													arms_factory > 0
													NOT = { state = PREV.PREV }
													NOT = { state = PREV.PREV.PREV.PREV }
												}
												damage_building = {
													type = arms_factory
													damage = 0.9
												}
												if = {
													limit = {
														dockyard > 0
													}
													damage_building = {
														type = dockyard
														damage = 0.9
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						25 = {}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					60 = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.3 } }
					25 = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.2 } }
					15 = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.2 } }
				}
				random_list = {
					52 = {
						add_to_variable = { var = central_mojave_intensity value = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_increases
					}
					48 = {}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 10 } }
				#secession_raid_crisis = yes # Calls the scripted effect to launch a secession crisis
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = "Something has gone really fucking wrong - tell @HappyNTH"
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {

		}

	enlargen_garrison_central_mojave = {
		priority = 8
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				central_mojave_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = central_mojave_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = central_mojave_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_central_mojave
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { central_mojave_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_central_mojave }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_central_mojave
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = central_mojave_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { central_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { central_mojave_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { central_mojave_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { central_mojave_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { central_mojave_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_central_mojave
		}
	}

	raider_pulse_northern_mojave = {
		priority = 7
		activation = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_intensity = 0 } }

				northern_mojave_raid_district = yes
			}
			OR = {
				tag = NCR

	enlargen_garrison_northern_mojave = {
		priority = 6
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				northern_mojave_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = northern_mojave_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = northern_mojave_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_northern_mojave
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_northern_mojave }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_northern_mojave
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = northern_mojave_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { northern_mojave_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_northern_mojave
		}
	}

				custom_effect_tooltip = if_ncr_agrees_rangers

					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 6 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 5 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_rangers
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_rangers } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }
						subtract_from_variable = { northern_mojave_intenisty = 6 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity
					}
					else = {

						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
					}
				}

			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_northern_mojave
		}

	enlargen_garrison_baja = {
		priority = 4
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				baja_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = baja_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = baja_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_baja
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { baja_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = baja_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { baja_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja
		}
	}

	arm_civilians_baja = {
		priority = 4
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				baja_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = baja_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = baja_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_baja
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { baja_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = baja_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { baja_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { baja_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja
		}
	}

	# Call-and-Respond for puppets
	call_in_ncr_baja = {
		priority = 4
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				baja_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = baja_district_pacified }
			is_puppet_of = NCR
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = intensity_over_5
				check_variable = { baja_intensity > 5 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja }
			}
		}
		cost = 20
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja
			add_autonomy_score = {
			    value = -200
			    localization = called_in_ncr_military
			}
			NCR = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.4 days = 5 } }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = if_ncr_agrees_mil

							}

								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_list = {
							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
							15 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 4 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_4_intensity
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_mil
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund } }
						random_list = {
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 2 }

							}
							35 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 3 }

							}
						}

							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 3 }

							}

								subtract_from_variable = { baja_intenisty = 4 }

				NCR = { check_variable = { ranger_deployments > 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja }
			}
			has_manpower > 200
			has_200_weapons = yes
		}
		cost = 20
		days_remove = 20
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_baja
			subtract_from_variable = { ranger_deployments = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_deployment
			add_manpower = -200
			remove_200_weapons = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity

			}
