	enlargen_garrison_ranchers = {
		priority = 2
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				ranchers_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ranchers_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ranchers_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_ranchers
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { ranchers_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ranchers_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers
		}
	}

	arm_civilians_ranchers = {
		priority = 2
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				ranchers_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ranchers_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ranchers_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_ranchers
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { ranchers_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ranchers_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers
		}
	}
	employ_mercs_ranchers = {
		priority = 2
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				ranchers_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ranchers_district_pacified }
			has_global_flag = ncr_chose_big_jim
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost - purposefully one under so can be selected at that threshold
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ranchers_merc_use } }
				has_political_power > 19
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 } }
				has_political_power > 39
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 2 } }
				has_political_power > 79
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 3 } }
				has_political_power > 159
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 4 } }
				has_political_power > 319
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_pp_ranchers
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { ranchers_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = merc_limit_ranchers
				NOT = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 40
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ranchers_merc_use } }
					add_political_power = -20
					set_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 } }
					add_political_power = -40
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 2 } }
					add_political_power = -80
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 3 } }
					add_political_power = -160
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 4 } }
					add_political_power = -320
					add_to_variable = { ranchers_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 2 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
				}
				25 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 3 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
				} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_ranchers
		}
	}

							}

								subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 4 }

							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_mil

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }

						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund } }

							65 = {

						}

							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { ranchers_intenisty = 3 }

	enlargen_garrison_nevada = {
		priority = 0
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				nevada_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = nevada_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = nevada_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_nevada
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { nevada_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = nevada_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { nevada_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { nevada_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { nevada_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { nevada_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { nevada_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada
		}
	}
	attempt_integration_nevada = {
		priority = 0

			}
		}
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 100
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				60 = {} # No effect
				35 = {

	arm_civilians_nevada = {
		priority = 0
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				nevada_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = nevada_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = nevada_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_nevada
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { nevada_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = nevada_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { nevada_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nevada_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_nevada
		}

					add_to_variable = { nevada_merc_use = 1 }

					add_to_variable = { nevada_merc_use = 1 }

					add_political_power = -320
					add_to_variable = { nevada_merc_use = 1 }
				}

	raider_pulse_junktown = {

		activation = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_intensity = 0 } }

				is_puppet_of = NCR
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = @junktown_pulse
		is_good = no
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

	enlargen_garrison_junktown = {
		priority = -2
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				junktown_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = junktown_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = junktown_garrison_use } }
				has_manpower > 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 } }
				has_manpower > 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 2 } }
				has_manpower > 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 3 } }
				has_manpower > 200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 4 } }
				has_manpower > 400
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_manpower_junktown
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = garrison_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 100
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = junktown_garrison_use } }
					add_manpower = -25
					set_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 } }
					add_manpower = -50
					add_to_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 2 } }
					add_manpower = -100
					add_to_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 3 } }
					add_manpower = -200
					add_to_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 4 } }
					add_manpower = -400
					add_to_variable = { junktown_garrison_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund }
				random_list = {
					80 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 3 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
					}
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 2 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_100_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
		}
	}

	arm_civilians_junktown = {
		priority = -2
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				junktown_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = junktown_district_pacified }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = junktown_arms_use } }
				has_50_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 } }
				has_100_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 2 } }
				has_200_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 3 } }
				has_400_weapons = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 4 } }
				has_800_weapons = yes
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_weapons_junktown
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = arms_limit
				NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = junktown_arms_use } }
					remove_50_weapons = yes
					set_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 } }
					remove_100_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 2 } }
					remove_200_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 3 } }
					remove_400_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 4 } }
					remove_800_weapons = yes
					add_to_variable = { junktown_arms_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_1_intensity
				}
				30 = {} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
		}
	}
	employ_mercs_junktown = {
		priority = -2
		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				junktown_raid_district = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = junktown_district_pacified }
			has_global_flag = ncr_chose_big_jim
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { # Scales the cost - purposefully one under so can be selected at that threshold
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = junktown_merc_use } }
				has_political_power > 19
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 1 } }
				has_political_power > 39
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 2 } }
				has_political_power > 79
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 3 } }
				has_political_power > 159
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 4 } }
				has_political_power > 319
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = raid_crisis_scaling_pp_junktown
		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if the intensity is 0
				tooltip = has_some_intensity
				NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_intensity = 0 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { # Prevents it being clicked if it has been used 5 times
				tooltip = merc_limit_junktown
				NOT = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 5 } }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = not_taking_anti_raider_action
				NOT = { has_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown }
			}
		}
		days_remove = 40
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
			hidden_effect = {

					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 1 } }
					add_political_power = -40
					add_to_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 2 } }
					add_political_power = -80
					add_to_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 3 } }
					add_political_power = -160
					add_to_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 4 } }
					add_political_power = -320
					add_to_variable = { junktown_merc_use = 1 }
				}
				else = {} # Should never happen
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 2 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
				}
				25 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 3 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
				} # No effect
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = return_in_60_days
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
		}

	call_in_ncr_junktown = {
		priority = -2
		visible = {

			    value = -200
			    localization = called_in_ncr_military
			}
			NCR = { country_event = { id = raid_trouble.4 days = 5 } }

			if = {

						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund } }

								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							35 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_list = {
							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
							15 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 4 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_4_intensity
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_mil
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_drummund } }
						random_list = {
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							35 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_list = {
							20 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 2 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_2_intensity
							}
							65 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 3 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_3_intensity
							}
							15 = {
								subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 4 }
								custom_effect_tooltip = lose_4_intensity
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ncr_refuses_mil
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown

	call_rangers_junktown = {

					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 5 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ncr_refuses_rangers
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ncr_refuses_rangers } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ncr_chose_mossman } }
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 6 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_6_intensity
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { junktown_intenisty = 5 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = lose_5_intensity
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ncr_refuses_rangers
			clr_country_flag = taking_anti_raider_action_junktown
		}
	}
